  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_1c45e10f-3142-4e5d-ab2d-cf34e62dd558'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initializeSiwa();

<div id="descriptionContainer">
  
      <div id="description" class="readable stacked" style="right:0">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer17558336999375786239">After a research facility is destroyed, the surrounding forest becomes a horrific war zone between intelligent winged mutants and mercenaries hired by the man that created them. When a mutant infects a local, Sarah's cancer is cured and both sides discover that she holds the key to their future.<br/><br/>Richard Myerscough's Bat Blood contains common themes found in techno-thrillers</span>
  <span id="freeText17558336999375786239" style="display:none">After a research facility is destroyed, the surrounding forest becomes a horrific war zone between intelligent winged mutants and mercenaries hired by the man that created them. When a mutant infects a local, Sarah's cancer is cured and both sides discover that she holds the key to their future.<br /><br />Richard Myerscough's Bat Blood contains common themes found in techno-thrillers like Michael Critchton's Prey, medical thriller's such as Robin Cook's Coma, and horror/sci/fi in the same vein as John Saul's The God Project.<br /> Bat Blood is a fun novel that contains cinematic battle scenes that might have come out of a Michael Bay action movie.<br /> What makes the novel even more frightening, beyond just the fear of the unknown, is that it feels as though the content could be ripped out of the latest newspaper headlines.<br /> Clarion Review<br /><br />Sarah's cure was her curse, and her destiny<br /><br /> After Sarah Douglas is attacked and infected with the blood of a gargoyle-like creature, the cancer that riddled her body vanishes. The attack draws the attention of Doctor Scott, the scientist who inadvertently was responsible for infecting a colony of bats, and changing them into intelligent creatures that could threaten mankind.<br /><br /> As the infected blood slowly transforms Sarah's body, she is caught in the middle of an horrific war between an army of mercenaries and a colony of mutate winged creatures. Watching the creatures gorge themselves on human flesh, she sees her future and fights to maintain her humanity.<br /><br /> With Sarah's blood holding the key to his research the doctor uses his vast resources to try to capture her, along with keeping the outside world at bay. This gets harder to do as the colony expands its territory further away from the Devil's Claw, and members of the local population begin to disappear.</span>

      </div>

  <span id="freeText15154200362798908875" style="display:none">First, I want to thank Mr. Richard Myerscough for giving me the opportunity to read his book. This book had it all, a little romance, suspense, drama and a boat-load of action. I thoroughly enjoyed the way things unfolded and what made it even more real is the fact that it was dipped heavily in stem-cell research. This was a "rollercoaster" of a ride and I will definitely be reading the 2nd part of the series as well. I recommend fans of horror/action to check out this exciting book when given the first opportunity. You won't be disappointed.</span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3196244926" />
    <a title="Dylan Derby" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/87153965-dylan-derby"><img alt="Dylan Derby" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/u_50x66-632230dc9882b4352d753eedf9396530.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3196244926?book_show_action=true">Feb 18, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dylan Derby" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dylan Derby" href="/user/show/87153965-dylan-derby">Dylan Derby</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3196244926" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4181454559838302139">I really wanted to love this book. The premise and such were tailor made for me to really enjoy this book, and yet it fell completely flat. Richard's writing comes off wooden and I truly believe besides maybe 2 or 3 characters in the book, everyone else has no real personality or anything. you could just take one character and replace them with another and you would have no idea that, that had even happened. the ending is a total blood bath of carnage and action but by that point nobody mattered</span>
  <span id="freeText4181454559838302139" style="display:none">I really wanted to love this book. The premise and such were tailor made for me to really enjoy this book, and yet it fell completely flat. Richard's writing comes off wooden and I truly believe besides maybe 2 or 3 characters in the book, everyone else has no real personality or anything. you could just take one character and replace them with another and you would have no idea that, that had even happened. the ending is a total blood bath of carnage and action but by that point nobody mattered to me at all, most of the characters were nameless soldiers who most wind up getting killed in the same way as each other. I think my very high hopes for this book are why it fell so short for me. The characters are all wooden copies of each other with no real personalities and most of them don't even matter. In the entire book I truly was only interested in one character. Sarah the main character who is a child and turning into a monster is so terribly written I did not care about her at all and frankly she is not even the slightest bit believeable in her role in the novel. Pretty big let down to be honest. will not read the sequel.</span>
  <a data-text-id="4181454559838302139" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/551463842" />
    <a title="Laurie Wainwright" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/18020231-laurie-wainwright"><img alt="Laurie Wainwright" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/551463842?book_show_action=true">Mar 03, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Laurie Wainwright" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Laurie Wainwright" href="/user/show/18020231-laurie-wainwright">Laurie Wainwright</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback " href="/book/show/17385364-bat-blood">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Anyone that likes horror-thrillers</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18020231-laurie-wainwright?shelf=dark-action-thriller">dark-action-thriller</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer551463842" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6278213725790784100">It is not like any other vampire or creature books that I've ever read before.<br/>The author's unique way of giving the reader an insight into the creatures' lives, makes you almost want to pity the grotesque creatures that feel humans are nothing more than meat.<br/>As the main character Sarah slowly changes and is hunted down by the men hired by the medical researchers, her family is caught in the middle and must come to terms with what she is turning into. This meant a lot of bouncing around in the bo</span>
  <span id="freeText6278213725790784100" style="display:none">It is not like any other vampire or creature books that I've ever read before.<br />The author's unique way of giving the reader an insight into the creatures' lives, makes you almost want to pity the grotesque creatures that feel humans are nothing more than meat.<br />As the main character Sarah slowly changes and is hunted down by the men hired by the medical researchers, her family is caught in the middle and must come to terms with what she is turning into. This meant a lot of bouncing around in the book, however it also added another emotional aspect to the book. <br />I also appreciated the way the book went deeper into how the governing bodies that oversee medical research, the police and the environmental groups, were all taken into account. By showing how a group could manipulate them, the author demonstrates how plausible the science behind the book could be.<br />I highly recommend this book to anyone that likes a good edge of the seat read.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="6278213725790784100" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('bqhrNoioB6Y1Vfa2FdgdGb2k6kW1TezMDKkrUl1ZWd9s+VXhNk6YuYogfTPdYe9KgSJJRLcc89i9A/CPcLzOLA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

FACE OF THE EARTH is fiction, but all of the scientific and U.S. policy information in the novel has been scrupulously fact-checked.
